                                                                                      PEANUT ESIM · DELAWARE LLC DEEP DIVE

                                                                                      Understanding the Delaware LLC.

                                                                                      デラウェアLLCの構造を理解する。

                                                                                      Why it exists, how it's structured, how it makes us effectively tax-free, what we owe each year, and how to actually file it. Built so you and Akito both understand the entire structure before we incorporate.

                                                                                      なぜ存在するのか、どう構成されているか、どうやって実質的に非課税になるのか、毎年何を払うのか、実際の設立手続き — Balraj と Akito の両方が、設立前に全体構造を理解できるようまとめた解説。

                                                                                      01 / MENTAL MODEL01 / 全体イメージ

                                                                                      A legal wrapper around your business.

                                                                                      事業を包む「法的なラッパー」。

                                                                                      The LLC is a separate legal entity. You own 100% of it, but legally it's not you — it signs contracts, holds bank accounts, holds Stripe, owns the customer relationships. If something goes wrong, the LLC takes the hit, not your personal assets. LLC は、あなたとは別の独立した法人格を持つ「法人」です。あなたが 100% を保有しますが、法的にはあなた個人ではない — LLC が契約を結び、銀行口座を保有し、Stripe を保有し、顧客との関係を所有する。トラブルが起きても、LLC が責任を負い、あなたの個人資産は守られる。

                                                                                      You — Balraj (UAE resident) あなた — Balraj（UAE 居住者）
                                                                                      owns 100%100% を保有
                                                                                      Peanut eSIM LLC (Delaware)
                                                                                      ownsが所有
                                                                                      Mercury bank accountMercury 銀行口座 Stripe US Contracts契約 IP Customer data顧客データ Vendor relationships取引先関係

                                                                                      Three layers: You at the top (UAE resident, 0% personal income tax), the LLC in the middle (Delaware corporate entity), and the business assets at the bottom. The LLC sits between you and the operations like a shield. 3つの層: 最上層にあなた（UAE 居住者、個人所得税 0%）、中央に LLC（デラウェア法人）、最下層に事業資産。LLC がシールドとなり、あなたと事業オペレーションを隔てている。

                                                                                      02 / WHY DELAWARE02 / なぜデラウェア州なのか

                                                                                      Five reasons it's the standard.

                                                                                      5つの理由で業界標準。

                                                                                      Over 60% of Fortune 500 companies and nearly all US startups incorporate in Delaware. It's the most predictable, investor-friendly, and tax-efficient state for a non-resident-owned LLC. フォーチュン500企業の60%以上、米国スタートアップの大多数がデラウェア州で設立されている。米国非居住者所有 LLC にとって、最も予測可能・投資家フレンドリー・税効率が高い州。

                                                                                      Specialized business court専門ビジネス裁判所

                                                                                      The Court of Chancery handles only business disputes, with judges (not juries) trained in corporate law. Predictable, fast resolution — investors love this.Court of Chancery は商事紛争のみを扱う専門裁判所。陪審員ではなく企業法専門の裁判官が判断。予測可能・迅速な解決 — 投資家が好む理由。

                                                                                      Investor familiarity投資家の理解度

                                                                                      VCs and angels know Delaware law cold. If we ever raise capital, "Delaware LLC" or "Delaware C-Corp" is the default expectation — no friction.VC・エンジェル投資家はデラウェア州法を熟知。資金調達する場合、「デラウェア LLC」「デラウェア C-Corp」が標準前提 — 摩擦ゼロ。

                                                                                      Member privacyメンバーのプライバシー

                                                                                      Members (owners) don't appear in public records. Delaware doesn't publish member names — only the registered agent's address. Your name stays out of public databases.メンバー（オーナー）は公的記録に表示されない。デラウェアは登録代理人の住所のみ公開し、メンバー名は非公開。あなたの名前は公的データベースに残らない。

                                                                                      No state tax on non-DE operationsデラウェア外事業は州税ゼロ

                                                                                      If your business doesn't physically operate in Delaware (no office, no employees there), Delaware charges 0% state income tax. We operate from UAE → no state tax.事業がデラウェア州内で物理的に運営されていなければ（オフィスなし、従業員なし）、州所得税 0%。我々は UAE から運営 → 州税ゼロ。

                                                                                      Lowest annual fee年間費用が最安

                                                                                      $300 flat franchise tax per year for LLCs. Wyoming and Nevada are cheaper but lack the legal-system depth + investor signal. Worth the ~$300 premium.LLC のフランチャイズ税は年 $300 固定。Wyoming や Nevada はもう少し安いが、法制度の深さ・投資家への信号で劣る。約 $300 のプレミアムを払う価値あり。

                                                                                      03 / THE TAX MAGIC03 / 課税構造の核心

                                                                                      The "disregarded entity" sleight of hand.

                                                                                      「Disregarded Entity」という仕掛け。

                                                                                      This is the single most important concept to understand. A single-member LLC owned by a non-US person is treated by the IRS as a "disregarded entity" — meaning the LLC files an informational form, but pays zero US federal income tax. Income passes through to you, the owner. Because you're a UAE tax resident, UAE tax law applies — and UAE has 0% personal income tax. Net effective tax: 0%. これが最も重要な概念。米国非居住者が所有するシングルメンバー LLC は、IRS（米国内国歳入庁）から 「Disregarded Entity（無視される実体）」 として扱われる — LLC は情報報告フォームを提出するが、米国連邦所得税は ゼロ。所得はオーナー（あなた）にパススルー。あなたは UAE 居住者なので UAE 税法が適用される — UAE の個人所得税は 0%。実効税率:0%。

                                                                                      1
                                                                                      Customer pays $15 retail (via Stripe US or Apple/Google in-app)顧客が小売価格 $15 を支払う（Stripe US または Apple/Google アプリ内課金経由）
                                                                                      ↓
                                                                                      2
                                                                                      Money enters Peanut eSIM LLC's Mercury bank account (US-based)資金が Peanut eSIM LLC の Mercury 銀行口座（米国所在）に着金
                                                                                      ↓ US federal corporate tax: 0% (disregarded entity)米国連邦法人税:0%（Disregarded Entity）
                                                                                      ↓ Delaware state income tax: 0% (no DE operations)デラウェア州所得税:0%（州内事業なし）
                                                                                      3
                                                                                      You access the money via Mercury debit card / wire to UAE personal bank / direct vendor paymentsあなたが Mercury デビットカード / UAE 個人銀行口座への送金 / 取引先への直接支払いで資金にアクセス
                                                                                      ↓ UAE personal income tax: 0%UAE 個人所得税:0%
                                                                                      ★
                                                                                      Net effective tax: 0%実効税率:0%
                                                                                      One important caveat:重要な注意点: If UAE Corporate Tax authorities determine the LLC has a "permanent establishment" in UAE (because management happens from your UAE laptop), they could try to tax it at 9%. Mitigations: use Mercury as primary operational account (not UAE bank), keep good records that the entity is US-based, use US registered agent. Same pattern Airalo and Nomad use without issue. UAE 法人税当局が、LLC が UAE 内に「恒久的施設（Permanent Establishment）」を持つと判断した場合（管理が UAE のラップトップから行われていることを理由に）、9% で課税しようとする可能性がある。対策:Mercury を主要運用口座として使用（UAE 銀行ではなく）、米国法人である記録を残す、米国登録代理人を使用。Airalo や Nomad が問題なく使っているのと同じパターン。

                                                                                      申し込みから稼働開始まで — 14〜21日。

                                                                                      06 / FORM 5472 EXPLAINED06 / Form 5472 の正体

                                                                                      It's a customs declaration, not a tax return.

                                                                                      これは税関申告書であって、税務申告ではない。

                                                                                      The single most confusing thing about Delaware LLCs is: "wait — I have to file a tax form every year?" Yes and no. It's filed through the tax-filing system, but it's not actually a tax return. Here's exactly what's going on. デラウェアLLCで最も誤解されるポイント:「毎年税務申告が必要なの？」答えは Yes でもあり No でもある。税務申告システムを通じて提出するが、実態は税務申告ではない。中身を説明します。

                                                                                      The customs-form analogy税関申告書のアナロジー

                                                                                      When you land in any country, you fill out a customs form. Even if you have nothing to declare and owe zero duty, you still have to write your name, flight number, and tick "Nothing to declare." You're not being taxed — you're being counted and tracked. どこかの国に到着したとき、税関申告書を書きます。申告するものがなく、関税ゼロでも、名前と便名を書いて「申告なし」にチェックし、職員に渡します。これは課税ではなく、記録と把握のための手続き。

                                                                                      Form 5472 is exactly the same. The US government wants a record that: Form 5472 はこれと全く同じ。米国政府が記録したいのは以下の3点:

                                                                                      • A US entity exists (your LLC)米国法人が存在する事実（あなたのLLC）
                                                                                      • It's owned by a foreigner (you)所有者が外国人であること（あなた）
                                                                                      • Here's how much money moved between you and the entity this year年間でオーナーと法人の間に動いた金額

                                                                                      No tax. Just a "here we are" piece of paper. 税金ゼロ。「ここに存在しています」という1枚の書類だけ。

                                                                                      Why is it called "Form 1120" if it's not a tax return?税務申告ではないのに、なぜ「Form 1120」と呼ばれるのか？

                                                                                      The US IRS only has one filing system — the corporate tax return (Form 1120). When they needed foreign-owned LLCs to disclose ownership info, they said: "File the regular corporate tax return, but leave most of it blank. Attach Form 5472 with the disclosure info." 米国IRSは法人税申告のシステムを1つしか持っていない（Form 1120）。外国人所有のLLCに所有情報を開示させる必要が出てきたとき、IRS はこう決めた:「通常の法人税申告書を提出してください。ただし大部分は空欄でOK。開示情報を記載した Form 5472 を添付してください」

                                                                                      That's why it's called "1120 pro-forma" — pro-forma means "placeholder / skeleton." The 1120 itself has nothing on it because there's no US tax to pay. It's just the envelope that delivers Form 5472. だから「1120 pro-forma」と呼ばれる — pro-forma は「形式的・骨組みだけ」の意味。1120 自体には何も記載しない（米国税金がゼロのため）。Form 5472 を届けるための「封筒」にすぎない。

                                                                                      What goes on the form vs. what doesn'tフォームに記載する情報・記載しない情報

                                                                                      ✅ GOES ON FORM 5472✅ Form 5472 に記載 ❌ DOES NOT GO ON FORM❌ フォームには記載しない
                                                                                      You wired $5K from Dubai to fund the LLC's startup costsドバイから $5K をLLCの初期費用として送金 Customer paid $15 for an eSIM plan顧客が eSIM プランに $15 を支払い
                                                                                      LLC wired $10K to your UAE personal bank as a distributionLLC があなたの UAE 個人口座に $10K を配当として送金 Stripe took $0.45 in feesStripe が $0.45 の手数料を徴収
                                                                                      You lent the LLC $20K, or the LLC lent you $20Kあなたが LLC に $20K 貸付、または逆方向 LLC paid wholesale supplier $5K wholesaleLLC が wholesale supplier に $5K の卸価格を支払い
                                                                                      LLC bought your laptop from you for $1KLLC があなたのラップトップを $1K で購入 LLC paid AWS / Vercel / hostingLLC が AWS / Vercel / ホスティングに支払い

                                                                                      TL;DR — in plain words要約（平易な言葉で）

                                                                                      "No tax owed. It's a once-a-year formality. We file a form that says: 'this LLC exists, it's owned by Balraj, and here's the money that moved between Balraj and the LLC this year.' That's it — no revenue reporting, no expense reporting. Just owner ↔ LLC transfers."

                                                                                      「税金ゼロ。年1回の形式的な手続き。『この LLC は存在する、オーナーは Balraj、今年 Balraj と LLC の間で動いた金額はこれだけ』という書類を提出するだけ。売上の報告も経費の報告もしない。オーナー ↔ LLC 間の資金移動の報告のみ」

                                                                                      07 / COMMON QUESTIONS07 / よくある質問

                                                                                      Things people get confused about.

                                                                                      混乱しがちなポイント。

                                                                                      Do I need to live in or visit the US?米国に住んだり、訪問する必要はある？
                                                                                      No. You never have to set foot in the US. Stripe Atlas handles everything remotely. Mercury bank opens entirely online. Stripe US can be operated from anywhere.不要。一度も米国に行く必要はない。Stripe Atlas が遠隔ですべて処理。Mercury 銀行口座も完全オンライン開設。Stripe US は世界中どこからでも運用可能。
                                                                                      Do I owe US income tax on the LLC's revenue?LLC の売上に対して米国所得税を払う必要は？
                                                                                      No. As long as you're a non-US person and the LLC has no "Effectively Connected Income" to a US trade or business (i.e., no US employees, no US office, no US-source business activity), no US federal tax. You file Form 5472 + 1120 pro-forma as informational only.不要。あなたが米国非居住者で、LLC が米国事業に「実質的に関連する所得（Effectively Connected Income）」を持たない限り（米国従業員なし、米国オフィスなし、米国源泉事業活動なし）、米国連邦税はゼロ。Form 5472 + 1120 pro-forma を情報報告のみ提出。
                                                                                      What if I sell to US customers — does that trigger US tax?米国の顧客に販売した場合、米国課税が発生する？
                                                                                      No. Selling digital goods to US consumers from your laptop in Dubai is not "Effectively Connected Income." US tax only triggers if you have substantial US operations (employees, office, physical inventory in US). Pure digital cross-border sales = no US tax.発生しない。Dubai のラップトップから米国消費者にデジタル商品を販売することは「Effectively Connected Income」に該当しない。米国課税は実質的な米国事業（従業員・オフィス・米国内在庫）がある場合のみ発生。純粋なデジタル越境販売は米国課税ゼロ。
                                                                                      Is Akito already a co-owner from day 1?Akito は最初から共同オーナーになる？
                                                                                      Yes — locked 2026-05-24. LLC is multi-member from incorporation. Both Balraj and Akito are legal co-owners (~50/50). The LLC files Form 1065 (partnership return) + K-1s annually. Both members need a US ITIN (Form W-7) — see Phase 1 Item 19. This replaces the earlier single-member assumption.確定 2026-05-24。LLC は設立時から複数構成員。Balraj と Akito の両者が法的共同所有者（~50/50）。LLC は毎年 Form 1065（パートナーシップ申告書）+ K-1 を提出。両メンバーに米国 ITIN（Form W-7）が必要 — Phase 1 Item 19 参照。以前のシングルメンバー想定は廃止。
                                                                                      What about UAE Corporate Tax (the new 9%)?UAE の法人税（新設の 9%）はどうなる？
                                                                                      UAE Corporate Tax applies to UAE-incorporated entities with taxable income above AED 375K. Our LLC is incorporated in Delaware, so it's a foreign entity. UAE Corporate Tax doesn't apply unless UAE deems the LLC has a "permanent establishment" in UAE (which we mitigate via US bank, US registered agent, US payment processor). Same exact pattern Airalo and Nomad use without issue.UAE 法人税は UAE 設立法人 で課税所得が AED 375K を超える場合に適用される。我々の LLC は デラウェア州 で設立されるため、外国法人。UAE が LLC を UAE 内の「恒久的施設」とみなさない限り、UAE 法人税は適用されない（米国銀行、米国登録代理人、米国決済代行を使うことで対策）。Airalo や Nomad が問題なく使っているのと同じパターン。
                                                                                      What's the difference between LLC and C-Corp?LLC と C-Corp の違いは？
                                                                                      LLC: simpler, more flexible, pass-through taxation by default (best for our case). C-Corp: taxed at 21% federal corporate tax, but preferred by US VCs raising priced rounds. We start with LLC and convert to C-Corp later only if we raise venture funding.LLC:シンプル、柔軟、デフォルトでパススルー課税（我々の用途に最適）。C-Corp:連邦法人税 21% が発生するが、プライストラウンドを行う米国 VC が好む形態。まず LLC で開始し、VC 資金調達時のみ後で C-Corp に変換する流れ。

                                                                                      How to actually file it.

                                                                                      実際の申請方法。

                                                                                      Three viable paths. For our case, Stripe Atlas wins on every dimension. 3つの選択肢。我々のケースではあらゆる点で Stripe Atlas が最適。

                                                                                      METHOD方法 COST費用 TIMELINE期間 PROS / CONS長所 / 短所
                                                                                      Stripe Atlas ⭐ $500 flat 2–3 weeks All-in-one (LLC + EIN + Mercury + Stripe + templates + $5K Stripe credit). Designed for non-US founders. Best fit for us.オールインワン（LLC + EIN + Mercury + Stripe + テンプレート + $5K Stripe クレジット）。非米国居住者向け設計。最適。
                                                                                      Firstbase $399 2–3 weeks Similar to Atlas, slightly cheaper. Bank options narrower. Smaller community.Atlas と類似、やや安価。銀行選択肢が狭い。コミュニティ規模が小さい。

                                                                                      DIY (file direct)自分で申請 ~$150 4–8 weeks Cheapest, slowest. You handle EIN application + Mercury opening + Stripe underwriting separately. High learning curve for non-US founders.最安、最遅。EIN 申請 + Mercury 開設 + Stripe アンダーライティングを個別対応。非米国居住者には学習コスト高い。

                                                                                      PEANUT ESIM · PRICING, BEHAVIOR & ECONOMICS ARCHITECTURE

                                                                                      Pricing, Behavior & Economics Architecture — every plan, every decision, every assumption.

                                                                                      プライシング・行動・経済アーキテクチャ — 全プラン、全意思決定、全前提

                                                                                      The full strategic walk-through behind Peanut's 7-tier ladder (Tab 1), the behavioral model that predicts how crew actually consume data (Tab 2), and the per-user unit economics that translate prices + behavior into profit (Tab 3). Cabin-class pricing logic, geo cost buckets, mix assumptions, operating cost, the backdoor exploits we closed — plus the 4 user archetypes, per-tier consumption rates, the 1-GB refill UX insight, and the locked per-user profit math for every tier. What's locked, why, and what's still open. Last updated 2026-06-01.

                                                                                      Peanut の7段階ティア戦略を支える全ロジック (Tab 1)、乗務員データ消費の行動モデル (Tab 2)、そしてプライス×行動を利益に変換するユーザー単位経済モデル (Tab 3) の完全解説。キャビンクラス価格論理、地域別コスト、ユーザー構成比、運営コスト、塞いだ抜け穴、4つのユーザー類型、ティア別消費率、1GBリフィルUXの洞察、各ティアのユーザー1人あたり利益。確定事項、根拠、残課題。最終更新 2026-06-01。

                                                                                      This document captures the full reasoning and locked decisions behind Tab 1 (Pricing Architecture), Tab 2 (User Behavior), and Tab 3 (Per-Tier Unit Economics) of the Peanut eSIM P&L Model. Tab 1 sets every retail price, pool size, carryover rule, cost bucket, mix percentage, and operating cost line. Tab 2 predicts how much of that pool crew will actually USE — the intelligence layer that drives COGS, gross margin, LTV, and breakage downstream. Tab 3 then translates prices + behavior into a single per-user profit number for each tier — the bridge between architecture and money. Together they form the foundation the rest of the 16-tab model pivots from. Built once, never re-litigate.

                                                                                      TAB 1タブ1

                                                                                      Updated 2026-06-02最終更新 2026-06-02

                                                                                      UPDATE 2026-06-01 — Geo cost mix revised to Emirates-realistic

                                                                                      The Tier-A / Tier-B / Tier-C mix has been recalibrated from 60/25/15 to 75/20/5 to reflect Emirates crew's actual concentration on Asia + Europe + USA destinations (Tier-A) rather than even-weighted layovers. This drops the blended wholesale cost from $2.13/GB to $1.34/GB. Downstream per-tier wholesale references previously held at $1.20 (conservative placeholder) are now updated to $1.34. All per-tier economics and Logic tabs reflect the revised cost. Retail prices are unchanged.

                                                                                      1. What this architecture is and why it matters

                                                                                      Tab 1 is the master input sheet of the entire 16-tab P&L model. Every downstream calculation — Tab 3 (Per-Tier Unit Economics), Tab 4 (Volume Scenarios), Tab 6 (24-Month Rollout), Tab 8 (LTV-CAC), Tab 10 (Carryover Liability), Tab 11 (Strategic Scenarios), Tab 12 (Cash + Sensitivity) — references the cells in Tab 1. Change one number here, the whole model recalculates.

                                                                                      The architecture has five sections, top to bottom:

                                                                                      #SectionWhat it controls
                                                                                      1Color KeyVisual legend for the model — what cell colors mean
                                                                                      2Cabin Class Retail PricesThe 7-tier price ladder — every plan's price, pool, carry rules
                                                                                      3Geo Cost BucketsWholesale cost per GB by country bucket (drives our COGS)
                                                                                      4Cabin-Class Mix% of paying users on each tier (drives blended ARPU)
                                                                                      5Operating Cost / User / MonthWhat we pay per active user beyond data (Stripe fees, support, cloud)

                                                                                      2. Section 1 — Color Key

                                                                                      Visual conventions used throughout the model:

                                                                                      ColorMeaning
                                                                                      Blue textHardcoded input — change at will
                                                                                      Black textFormula — do not edit
                                                                                      Green textCross-sheet reference (pulled from another tab)
                                                                                      Yellow fillKey assumption — review before pitching

                                                                                      3. Section 2 — Cabin Class Retail Prices (the locked ladder)

                                                                                      This is the single most important section in the entire workbook. Every revenue calculation downstream pivots from these 7 rows. Below are the locked prices, the reasoning, and the deep-dive on each tier (each plan has its own dedicated "Logic" tab in the workbook).

                                                                                      2.1 Economy (PAYG)

                                                                                      FieldValue
                                                                                      Price$4.99 per 1 GB top-up
                                                                                      Pool1 GB per purchase
                                                                                      Subscription?NO — single-purchase, no recurring charge
                                                                                      Coverage (v1)Flat worldwide (zonal in v1.1)
                                                                                      CarryoverNone — unused data expires with the top-up
                                                                                      StatusLocked

                                                                                      The 5-layer pricing logic behind $4.99

                                                                                      LayerRationale
                                                                                      1. Cost floorwholesale supplier's actual wholesale (real rate sheet) for 1-GB short-trip plans: $0.56–1.25/GB in cheap zones (HK/Korea/Japan/Singapore/USA/UK). At $4.99 retail = 75-89% gross margin on typical crew trips.
                                                                                      2. Market middleAiralo 1 GB / 7-day USA ~$4.50, Roamless ~$4.00, Crew SIM $3-7 depending on country. We sit in the fair-middle, not the discount race.
                                                                                      3. PsychologicalUnder-$5 = impulse purchase zone. $5.99 = considered purchase. The 9-cents rule matters here.
                                                                                      4. Upsell anchor3 top-ups in a month = $14.97 → that's more than Premium Economy ($17.99 for 10 GB). The user does the math, upgrades.
                                                                                      5. Crew fit1 GB matches 1 layover. Selling 10 GB to a 1-trip crew traveler feels wasteful → churn risk.

                                                                                      Flat vs Zonal decision

                                                                                      Locked: Flat $4.99 worldwide for v1. Zonal pricing for India/Brazil/Africa in v1.1 (3-6 months post-launch).

                                                                                      Why flat: "Pay $5 anywhere you fly" is a clean marketing line. The ~10% of crew trips that happen in loss-making zones (India/Brazil/South Africa) are subsidized by the 90% in cheap zones (Asia/Europe/USA). At 10K Economy users, the worst-case loss is ~$2K/mo, dwarfed by $38K/mo profit from healthy zones. Net: +$36K/mo, defensible.

                                                                                      Backdoor closure

                                                                                      Economy is blocked for active subscribers in the app. Without this, a Business user paying $29.99/mo for 15 GB could buy 5 Economy top-ups at $4.99/GB instead of refueling at the old $5.99/GB — and save money. We close this by hiding Economy from subscribers entirely.

                                                                                      2.2 Roster Bundle

                                                                                      FieldValue
                                                                                      Price$3.99 per flight bundled, capped at $39.99/month
                                                                                      Pool modelPer-flight, not pool-based — separate country-specific eSIMs bundled together
                                                                                      Auto-armingYES — eSIM activates when crew lands at each city
                                                                                      Discount vs Economy$1/flight saved (20% off the $4.99 PAYG rate)
                                                                                      Subscription?Monthly recurring once enrolled — auto-renews on next roster upload
                                                                                      StatusLocked

                                                                                      The fundamental insight that drove the design

                                                                                      A PAYG user with 5 scheduled flights in a month doesn't buy 5 SIMs. They buy 1-2 when they remember. Real PAYG behavior captures ~$8-11/mo per user. Roster Bundle's job is to capture the WHOLE month upfront — get the user to pre-commit to all 5 flights at a discount, lifting per-user revenue to $19.95 (5 × $3.99) with predictable cash flow.

                                                                                      5-flight worked example

                                                                                      Citywholesale supplier wholesale costPAYG price ($4.99)Bundle price ($3.99)
                                                                                      Tokyo$0.90$4.99$3.99
                                                                                      Singapore$0.83$4.99$3.99
                                                                                      London$1.25$4.99$3.99
                                                                                      Sydney$1.04$4.99$3.99
                                                                                      Mumbai$5.21$4.99$3.99
                                                                                      TOTAL$9.23$24.95$19.95

                                                                                      Why Bundle wins despite "lower" per-user profit vs full PAYG

                                                                                      Reality checkOutcome
                                                                                      PAYG user buys 2 of 5 (typical)$8.25 profit
                                                                                      PAYG user buys 3 of 5$11.48 profit
                                                                                      Bundle captures all 5 (locked-in)$10.72 profit + low support burden + low churn

                                                                                      Bundle captures users who would otherwise drop out mid-month. Revenue per user roughly doubles vs PAYG.

                                                                                      $39.99 monthly cap rationale

                                                                                      Heavy-flier crew (12+ flights/month) would otherwise pay $47.88+ at $3.99/flight. The cap at $39.99 makes Roster Bundle feel safe for heavy users — no fear of runaway billing. Margin compression on 12-flight users is acceptable for the loyalty + LTV gains.

                                                                                      2.3 Premium Economy

                                                                                      FieldValue
                                                                                      Price$17.99/month (was $12.99 placeholder)
                                                                                      Pool10 GB monthly
                                                                                      Carryover50% × 1 month
                                                                                      CoverageGlobal pool — works in any country on supplier network
                                                                                      Auto-armingNO — manual eSIM install
                                                                                      UX1-GB active at a time, manual refill from pool
                                                                                      PerksLounge guides
                                                                                      StatusLocked

                                                                                      Why the price was bumped from $12.99 to $17.99

                                                                                      The original $12.99 placeholder was cheaper than Roster Bundle ($19.95 for 5 flights). A crew member looking at the price card would see "Premium Economy is cheaper AND works anywhere" and choose it 100% of the time — cannibalizing Roster Bundle, which is the wedge feature.

                                                                                      $17.99 sits $2 below Roster Bundle, signaling "cheaper but you trade away auto-arming" — clean positioning, no cannibalization.

                                                                                      The 1-GB refill UX mechanic

                                                                                      Users see only 1 GB active at a time. When that GB runs out, they tap "Refill from pool" to get the next GB. The pool is always visible (transparency), but refill requires manual action.

                                                                                      Why this matters: friction-limited consumption drops from 62.5% (auto-deduct baseline) to ~40%. The unused 60% either rolls into carry or breaks. Pure breakage profit comes from forgetfulness, not deception.

                                                                                      Transparency policy (locked)

                                                                                      RuleReason
                                                                                      Pool is ALWAYS visibleNever hide what user paid for
                                                                                      Refill button is visible at all timesOne tap, no friction beyond explicit action
                                                                                      Day-25 reminder push: "You have X GB unused — refill?"Give them every chance to consume what they paid for
                                                                                      Carryover shown explicitly: "Y GB will carry, Z GB will expire"Honest disclosure
                                                                                      Breakage we earn from honest forgetfulness is fair revenue. Breakage we earn from hidden mechanics is fraud.

                                                                                      Per-user economics at $17.99

                                                                                      LineValue
                                                                                      Subscription revenue$17.99
                                                                                      GB consumed (40% friction)4.0 GB
                                                                                      Wholesale COGS at $1.34/GB blended$5.36
                                                                                      Gross profit (subscription)$12.63 (70% margin)
                                                                                      + Refuel (20% attach × $4.99)+$0.93 net
                                                                                      Total per user / mo$13.56 (71% margin)

                                                                                      2.4 Business ⭐ RECOMMENDED

                                                                                      FieldValue
                                                                                      Price$29.99/month (was $24.99 placeholder)
                                                                                      Pool15 GB monthly
                                                                                      Carryover70% × 1 month
                                                                                      UXSame 1-GB refill mechanic as Premium
                                                                                      PerksPriority support + crew recs unlocked
                                                                                      Tier flag"RECOMMENDED" on price card
                                                                                      PersonaSenior crew, full-rota crew, frequent travelers — the default subscriber
                                                                                      StatusLocked

                                                                                      The 5 reasons for $29.99 (not $24.99)

                                                                                      ReasonDetail
                                                                                      Meaningful upgrade gap$17.99 → $24.99 was only +$7. Felt like a small bump. +$12 to $29.99 signals "real upgrade."
                                                                                      Market roomAiralo at ~$50 for 20 GB. We're still significantly below the market ceiling.
                                                                                      Persona-fitBusiness buyers are typically senior crew with higher salaries. $5/mo is dinner money to them.
                                                                                      Promo headroomAt $29.99 we can run "first month $19.99" without bleeding margin. At $24.99 we'd have nothing to give.
                                                                                      Compounded upsideAt 100K users × 8% Business × +$5/mo = +$480K/year pure margin. Material upside from one decision.

                                                                                      Per-user economics at $29.99

                                                                                      LineValue
                                                                                      Subscription revenue$29.99
                                                                                      GB consumed (45% — heavier than Premium)6.75 GB
                                                                                      Wholesale COGS at $1.34/GB blended$9.05
                                                                                      Gross profit (subscription)$20.94 (70% margin)
                                                                                      + Refuel (25% attach)+$1.16 net
                                                                                      Total per user / mo$22.10 (70% margin)

                                                                                      2.5 First

                                                                                      FieldValue
                                                                                      Price$39.99/month
                                                                                      Pool25 GB monthly (was 20 GB in earlier draft)
                                                                                      Carryover100% × 2 months (longer carry = top-tier differentiator)
                                                                                      UXSame 1-GB refill mechanic
                                                                                      PerksConcierge layer (direct human support)
                                                                                      PersonaSenior crew wanting more pool than Business
                                                                                      StatusLocked

                                                                                      Why we created TWO First tiers (First + First Suite)

                                                                                      Original plan was a single First at $49.99 / 25 GB. But the gap from Business ($29.99 / 15 GB) to First ($49.99 / 25 GB) felt big and one-dimensional. Splitting into First $39.99/25GB and First Suite $49.99/40GB creates a clean ladder mirroring Emirates' actual cabin naming (First Class + First Class Suite). First captures purser-grade crew who feel above Business but not in "Suite" territory.

                                                                                      The 1-GB friction insight (locked-in understanding)

                                                                                      Pool expansion is essentially free to us. The 1-GB refill friction caps actual consumption at ~13-14 GB regardless of whether the pool is 15, 20, 25, or 40 GB. Bigger pool = better value perception, same COGS. This is why First's pool was bumped 20 → 25 GB without changing price.

                                                                                      2.6 First Suite

                                                                                      FieldValue
                                                                                      Price$49.99/month
                                                                                      Pool40 GB monthly (was 30 GB earlier)
                                                                                      Carryover100% × 2 months
                                                                                      Per-GB price$1.25/GB — best per-GB on the entire ladder
                                                                                      UXSame 1-GB refill mechanic
                                                                                      PerksConcierge support + crew recs + priority + status badge
                                                                                      PersonaTop of ladder — heaviest travelers, lead purser, frequent fliers who want the "best deal"
                                                                                      StatusLocked

                                                                                      Why First Suite is the anchor product

                                                                                      At $1.25/GB it's the cheapest unit price on the price card. That creates the "this is the best deal" pull. Even users who would have bought Business or First Lite see the math and reconsider. Anchor pricing 101 — make the top tier obviously valuable per-unit.

                                                                                      2.7 Cockpit

                                                                                      FieldValue
                                                                                      Price$299/year (annual prepay only — no monthly option)
                                                                                      Monthly equivalent$24.92/mo (for ladder display only)
                                                                                      Pool12 GB monthly
                                                                                      Carryover100% × 2 months
                                                                                      Emergency bank12 GB lifetime — REFRESHES ANNUALLY (locked Option A)
                                                                                      Lockin12 months. No mid-year cancellation or refunds.
                                                                                      Persona"You be the pilot of your year" — set it for a year, stop thinking
                                                                                      StatusLocked

                                                                                      Critical reframing — Cockpit is NOT pilot-occupation

                                                                                      Earlier the model treated Cockpit as a pilot-only tier. This was wrong. The name "Cockpit" means "you be the pilot of your own data" — i.e., you're in command of a year of worry-free connectivity. Any user (crew, ground staff, frequent traveler) can buy it.

                                                                                      Why annual lock-in is the structural differentiator

                                                                                      Cockpit's value propWhat it means
                                                                                      Pay once for the yearOne decision, never again
                                                                                      Schedule changes? Route changes?Doesn't matter — you're covered
                                                                                      Unscheduled trips, vacation, family travel?All covered
                                                                                      Sick of plan management?Cockpit is the answer

                                                                                      Why the emergency bank refreshes annually (Option A)

                                                                                      Option consideredVerdict
                                                                                      A — Refreshes annually (PICKED)Cleanest mental model. Strong renewal incentive. ~$2.88/user/year cost.
                                                                                      B — True lifetime (one-time)Punishes loyal customers. Anti-renewal.
                                                                                      C — Accumulates with 24 GB capComplex to communicate. Long-term subs build big unpredictable banks.

                                                                                      Per-user annual economics

                                                                                      LineValue
                                                                                      Annual revenue (prepaid upfront)$299.00
                                                                                      Annual pool capacity156 GB (144 monthly + 12 emergency)
                                                                                      Annual base COGS (12 × 7.2 GB × $1.34)$115.78
                                                                                      Emergency usage cost (20% × 12 × $1.34)$3.22
                                                                                      Total annual COGS$119.00
                                                                                      Annual profit per user$180.00 (60% margin)

                                                                                      2.8 Refuel (add-on)

                                                                                      FieldValue
                                                                                      Price$4.99 per 1 GB top-up (was $5.99 — dropped to match Economy)
                                                                                      Pool1 GB per refuel
                                                                                      Available toActive subscribers ONLY
                                                                                      CarryNone
                                                                                      StatusLocked

                                                                                      Why refuel price was dropped from $5.99 to $4.99

                                                                                      The original $5.99 refuel rate was a "subscriber tax" — subscribers paid more per GB than PAYG users for the same product. That was both unfair and created the Economy backdoor. By matching refuel to Economy ($4.99) AND blocking Economy for subscribers, we close the loophole transparently.

                                                                                      4. Section 3 — Geo Cost Buckets

                                                                                      The simplest section structurally, but the most consequential numerically. Three cost buckets group countries by wholesale cost; a weighted mix produces a single "blended $/GB" number that every downstream tab uses as COGS.

                                                                                      BucketCountries$/GB (locked wholesale supplier data)% of trips (Emirates-realistic, updated 2026-06-01)
                                                                                      Tier-A (cheap)JP, UK, SG, MY, HK, KR, US$0.85 (was $0.97 placeholder)75%
                                                                                      Tier-B (medium)CA, AU, NZ, VN, UAE$1.40 (was $1.50)20%
                                                                                      Tier-C (expensive)IN, BR, SA, ZA$8.50 (was $5.80 — actually worse than estimate)5%
                                                                                      Blended cost / GB$1.34 at current mix (was $2.13 at 60/25/15)100%

                                                                                      Update 2026-06-01 — mix recalibrated from 60/25/15 to 75/20/5

                                                                                      The original 60/25/15 placeholder was set before we had a clear view of Emirates-specific route concentration. Emirates crew overwhelmingly fly Asia + Europe + USA (Tier-A), with relatively few rotations to Tier-C (India/Brazil/South Africa). Reweighting to 75% Tier-A / 20% Tier-B / 5% Tier-C drops the blended wholesale cost from $2.13 → $1.34/GB — a 37% reduction in unit COGS that flows through every per-tier P&L line.

                                                                                      Key insight from the wholesale supplier data audit

                                                                                      Sampling the supplier's actual settlement prices for 1-GB short-trip plans revealed that Tier-C destinations are WORSE than we estimated (India: $5.21 for 2-day, South Africa: $10.00 for 2-day). This makes the mix re-weighting even more material — at 5% Tier-C the expensive bucket barely moves the blended number; at 15% it dominated.

                                                                                      The real lever is the % mix, not the bucket prices. Emirates crew don't fly evenly across all 67 layover countries — they concentrate on Asia + Europe + USA. The 75/20/5 mix is the Emirates-specific reality.

                                                                                      Why the mix is flagged, not locked

                                                                                      The Emirates_Crew_Layover_Countries.xlsx file lists 67 countries (Africa 22, Europe 23, Asia Pacific 16, Americas 6) — but it gives country COUNT, not FLIGHT FREQUENCY. Real Emirates flight share is heavily Asia/Europe/USA, but we don't have the route-level data to validate exact percentages.

                                                                                      Validation path: Akito to collect 5-10 sample crew rosters → derive actual flight distribution → update the mix with real data.

                                                                                      5. Section 4 — Cabin-Class Mix

                                                                                      What % of paying users sit on each tier. Drives blended ARPU.

                                                                                      Tier%SourceConfidence
                                                                                      Economy (PAYG)50%SaaS benchmark — typically 40-60% in PAYG/free tierMedium
                                                                                      Roster Bundle18%Estimate — wedge feature, expect 15-25% adoptionLow
                                                                                      Premium Economy13%SaaS subscription benchmark — entry tier 10-15%Medium
                                                                                      Business ⭐8%"Best value" tier captures 5-10% in tiered SaaSMedium
                                                                                      First3%Split arbitrarily from old "First 5%"Low
                                                                                      First Suite2%Split arbitrarilyLow
                                                                                      Cockpit3%Annual prepay tiers typically 2-5%Low
                                                                                      Refuel attach30%SaaS top-up behavior 20-40% in PAYG-creditsMedium

                                                                                      Honest assessment of confidence

                                                                                      Nothing about this distribution is specifically validated for "eSIM products sold to airline cabin crew." This is a niche of a niche of a niche — no public dataset exists for it. The numbers are informed by general SaaS benchmarks (RevenueCat, OpenView, ProfitWell) and travel-app conversion rates, applied with crew-vertical adjustments.

                                                                                      Sensitivity stress-test added to Tab 7

                                                                                      Tab 7 (Behavior Sensitivity) now contains 5 mix scenarios spanning pessimistic to optimistic. Blended ARPU range: $14.55 — $21.48 (current model sits at $17.52 = middle of range). This validates that the placeholder mix is in defensible territory.

                                                                                      6. Section 5 — Operating Cost per User per Month

                                                                                      Costs we pay per active user beyond wholesale data. These directly hit gross profit.

                                                                                      LineValueStatus
                                                                                      Cloud / API per user$0.15Placeholder, acceptable
                                                                                      Payment processing$1.20 (was $0.50 placeholder)Locked with 3-scenario range
                                                                                      Customer support amortized$0.30Flagged — should be phase-based
                                                                                      SMS / OTP / verification$0.05Placeholder, acceptable
                                                                                      Hosting + dev tools amortized$0.10Placeholder, acceptable
                                                                                      TOTAL OPEX (current)$1.80/user/moUp from $1.10 original

                                                                                      Why payment processing was the big change

                                                                                      The original $0.50 placeholder dramatically under-estimated Stripe + Apple IAP fees. Real calculation:

                                                                                      TierTransactions/moCost/user/mo
                                                                                      Economy PAYG (2.5 × $4.99)2.5$1.10
                                                                                      Premium Economy1.3$0.96
                                                                                      Business1.25$1.29
                                                                                      First Suite1$1.75
                                                                                      Weighted blended~$1.00 Stripe-only / $1.20 mixed / $1.50 Apple IAP-heavy

                                                                                      3-scenario payment processing range

                                                                                      Scenario$/user/moAt 100K usersWhen to use
                                                                                      Optimistic (Stripe-only)$1.00$50K/moIf we route all iOS via web checkout
                                                                                      Realistic (mixed) ⭐$1.20$120K/moCURRENT MODEL VALUE
                                                                                      Conservative (IAP-heavy)$1.50$150K/moUse for investor pitches

                                                                                      What's still open in Section 5

                                                                                      • Customer support should be phase-based: $2-3/user pre-launch → $0.50 early scale → $0.15-0.20 at 100K+ users (currently flat $0.30)
                                                                                      • Fixed Monthly Burn is missing entirely: founder salaries, legal/accounting, insurance, marketing, software stack — needs a separate section (~$2K-25K/mo)

                                                                                      8. Backdoor exploits closed

                                                                                      #ExploitClosure
                                                                                      1Subscriber buys Economy ($4.99/GB) instead of refuel ($5.99/GB)Refuel dropped to $4.99 + Economy hidden from subscribers
                                                                                      2Business users downgrade to Cockpit per-GBAnnual lockin + emergency bank differentiates
                                                                                      3Refuel exploitRefuel matches Economy — fair, no advantage
                                                                                      4Roster heavy users shift to CockpitFair tradeoff — give up auto-arming for cheaper pool
                                                                                      5Premium vs Cockpit backdoorCockpit costs $83 more annually but bundles emergency + lockin

                                                                                      Validate cabin-class mix % with 20-30 crew interviewsAkitoHigh
